=== ALL POLICIES — 1505 total ===

ROLE-AWARE CLASSIFICATION. '-' = PUBLIC. service_role-only true-quals
are the normal explicit-access pattern (service_role bypasses RLS) and
are NOT counted as leaks.

=== SUMMARY ===
  CRITICAL cross-tenant READ leaks (broad role + USING(true) + has tenant_id): 274 policies on 246 tables
  Cross-tenant WRITE leaks (broad role + CHECK(true) + has tenant_id): 243 policies on 236 tables
  Broad-role true-qual on tables WITHOUT tenant_id (likely global/shared): 95
  anon INSERT-only capture endpoints (intentional): 2
  service_role-only true-quals (EXCLUDED, normal): 273
  suspicious (non-true, no scoping token): 63
